# Dialog Log

This file records interactive dialog between the **user** and **Claude Code** for this project.

It is intended as a chronological, append-only audit log:
- Each entry is timestamped (with timezone).
- User input and Claude responses are clearly labeled.
- New dialog entries are appended below the â€œLatest Dialogâ€ section.
- Older entries follow in chronological order.

This file may be updated automatically by local tooling.
It is not part of the public project history and may be excluded from the main branch.

[38;2;255;255;255mâº[39m I've reviewed the CLAUDE.md file. This is the OpenCV Pipeline Editor project - a JavaFX-based graphical node editor for building OpenCV image processing pipelines.

  Key points I'll follow:
  - [1mNo commits without explicit approval[22m - I'll suggest commits but wait for you to test and confirm
  - [1mNo claiming fixes work[22m - I'll say "I've made changes, please test" rather than asserting something is fixed
  - [1mBuild with [38;2;177;185;249mmvn compile[22m[39m to catch errors after changes

  The project also includes work on [1mccwrap[22m - a Python wrapper for Claude Code that adds journaling to DIALOG.md, email notifications when awaiting input, and Gmail polling for remote replies.

  What would you like to work on?

[38;2;255;255;255mâº[39m I've read the CLAUDE.md file. It contains project instructions for the [1mOpenCV Pipeline Editor[22m - a graphical node-based pipeline editor for OpenCV image processing operations.

  Key highlights:

  [1mImportant Policies:[22m
  - No git commits without explicit user approval
  - Don't claim fixes work until tested - use [38;2;177;185;249mmvn compile[39m to verify

  [1mBuild Commands:[22m
  - [38;2;177;185;249mmvn compile[39m - compile
  - [38;2;177;185;249mmvn exec:exec[39m - run normal
  - [38;2;177;185;249mmvn exec:exec@start[39m - run with auto-start
  - [38;2;177;185;249m./build-all-platforms.sh[39m - build release JARs for all platforms

  [1mTech Stack:[22m Java 17, JavaFX 23, OpenCV 4.9.0 (openpnp), Gson, Maven

  [1mAdding Processors:[22m Create a class in [38;2;177;185;249mfx/processors/[39m extending [38;2;177;185;249mFXProcessorBase[39m, add [38;2;177;185;249m@FXProcessorInfo[39m annotation, implement [38;2;177;185;249mprocess()[39m, [38;2;177;185;249mbuildPropertiesDialog()[39m, and serialization methods. Auto-discovered via annotation scanning.

  [1mSpecial Features:[22m
  - Raspberry Pi camera support via [38;2;177;185;249mrpicam-still[39m polling
  - Command line options for automation ([38;2;177;185;249m-a[39m, [38;2;177;185;249m--fullscreen_node_name[39m, [38;2;177;185;249m--max_time[39m, etc.)
  - Mat memory management with [38;2;177;185;249mMatTracker[39m

  [1mClaude Code Wrapper (ccwrap):[22m A Python tool in [38;2;177;185;249mtools/ccwrap/[39m that wraps Claude Code with:
  - Dialog journaling to [38;2;177;185;249mDIALOG.md[39m
  - Awaiting-user detection with email notifications
  - Git [38;2;177;185;249m_dialog[39m branch updates without checkout

  Would you like me to also read the README.md as recommended in the instructions?

[38;2;255;255;255mâº[39m I've read the README.md. Here are the key user-facing details:

  [1mWhat It Is:[22m A live visual node-based OpenCV pipeline editor where each node is an actual thread with queue-based connections between them. Supports sub-pipelines via containers.

  [1mQuick Start:[22m
  - Download platform-specific JAR from releases
  - Run: [38;2;177;185;249mjava -jar opencv-pipeline-<platform>.jar[39m
  - Auto-start: [38;2;177;185;249mjava -jar opencv-pipeline-<platform>.jar pipeline.json -a[39m
  - Requires Java 17+

  [1mPlatforms Supported:[22m
  - macOS Apple Silicon (M1-M5)
  - macOS Intel
  - Linux x86_64
  - Linux ARM64 (Raspberry Pi 4 & 5)
  - Windows x86_64
  - âŒ No Windows ARM64 (OpenCV limitation)

  [1mCommand Line Options:[22m
  - [38;2;177;185;249m-a[39m / [38;2;177;185;249m--auto_start[39m - auto-start pipeline
  - [38;2;177;185;249m--fullscreen_node_name NAME[39m - fullscreen preview
  - [38;2;177;185;249m--max_time SECONDS[39m - timed exit
  - Camera overrides: [38;2;177;185;249m--camera_index[39m, [38;2;177;185;249m--camera_resolution[39m, [38;2;177;185;249m--camera_fps[39m, [38;2;177;185;249m--camera_mirror[39m
  - Autosave behavior: [38;2;177;185;249m--autosave_prompt[39m, [38;2;177;185;249m--autosave_yes[39m, [38;2;177;185;249m--autosave_no[39m

  [1mRaspberry Pi CSI Cameras:[22m Automatic workaround using [38;2;177;185;249mrpicam-still[39m polling at ~10 fps. USB webcams recommended for higher frame rates (30+ fps).

  [1mKey Features:[22m 60+ processing nodes, real-time preview, threaded execution, container nodes for sub-pipelines, cross-platform.

  [1mKeyboard Shortcuts:[22m Delete, Ctrl+S/O/N for save/open/new, [1mF[22m for fullscreen preview

  [1mNode Categories:[22m Source, Color, Blur, Edge Detection, Morphological, Threshold, FFT, Detection, Transform, Drawing, Combine, Bitwise, Flow

  Ready to help with the project. What would you like to work on?
